
#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/leo/leo.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==4)
    {

 if(frame == 1){
   void self = getlocalvar("self");
   int PIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex");
   int HPs = getglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs");

   if(HPs!=NULL()){
     changeentityproperty(self, "health", HPs);
     setglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs", NULL());
   }
 }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==6)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");
    int mutated = getentityvar(self, 1);

    if(mutated != NULL() &&  mutated <= openborvariant("elapsed_time") - 3500){
      setentityvar(self, 1, NULL());
      performattack(self, openborconstant("ANI_PAIN9"));
    }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==7)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");
    int mutated = getentityvar(self, 1);

    if(mutated != NULL() &&  mutated <= openborvariant("elapsed_time") - 3500){
      setentityvar(self, 1, NULL());
      performattack(self, openborconstant("ANI_PAIN9"));
    }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==8)
    {

    void self = getlocalvar("self");
    int mutated = getentityvar(self, 1);

    if(mutated != NULL() &&  mutated <= openborvariant("elapsed_time") - 3500){
      setentityvar(self, 1, NULL());
      performattack(self, openborconstant("ANI_PAIN9"));
    }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==10)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 1);
    	}
    	else if (frame ==2){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==11)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");
	 if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            randSound("leo-turtle_power.wav", "leo_hehey.wav", "leo_hehey.wav");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==15)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 1);
    	}
    	else if (frame ==1){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==16)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index
	if(playerkeys(iPIndex, 0, "movedown")){// Down is pressed?
	performattack(self, openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW2"));
	}

   	else if( frame == 0){
      	int r = rand()%50;
      	if( r > 0){
        performattack(self, openborconstant("ANI_FOLLOW1"));
      	}
    	}
    	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==18)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            randSound("leo_pain.wav", "leo_pain02.wav", "leo_pain06.wav");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==19)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            randSound("leo_pain.wav", "leo_pain02.wav", "leo_pain06.wav");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==20)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==21)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==22)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
    int eTime = openborvariant("elapsed_time");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

     if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 1);
	changeentityproperty(Player, "direction", 1);
    	}
    	else if (frame ==6){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
      changeentityproperty(self, "invincible", 1);
      changeentityproperty(self, "invinctime", eTime + 200);
      changeentityproperty(self, "blink", 1);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==23)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==24)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==25)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            randSound("leo_fall02.wav", "leo_fall03.wav", "leo_fall02.wav");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==27)
    {
        if(frame==2)
        {
            randSound("leo_idontbelievethis.wav", "leo_idontbelievethis.wav", "leo_idontbelievethis.wav");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==28)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 1);
    	}
    	else if (frame ==3){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            randSound("leo_hiya2.wav", "leo_hiya2.wav", "leo_hiya2.wav");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==29)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 1);
    	}
    	else if (frame ==3){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==30)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index

    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 1);
    	}
    	else if (frame ==3){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==32)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index
    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

     if (frame ==0){
	changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
     if (frame ==20){
      	setdrawmethod(self, 1, 512, 512, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1);
	setentityvar(self, 1, openborvariant("elapsed_time"));
	
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            randSound("leo-turtle_power.wav", "leo_hehey.wav", "leo-turtle_power.wav");
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            spawnbind("mutagen_effect", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==33)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");


     if (frame ==0){
	changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
	setdrawmethod(self, 0);
    	}

	        return;
    }

}

      performattack(self, openborconstant("ANI_PAIN9"));
    }
        return;
    }

	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==408)
    {

 if(frame == 1){
   void self = getlocalvar("self");
   int PIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex");
   int HPs = getglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs");

   if(HPs!=NULL()){
     changeentityproperty(self, "health", HPs);
     setglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs", NULL());
   }
 }
        return;
    }

}

     setglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs", NULL());
   }
 }
        return;
    }

    	}

        }
        return;

void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==899)
    {
        if(frame==1)
        {
            spawn01("explosion_safe", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            spawnmerso("chrome_quake", 120, 0, 200);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

}

            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

}

    	}
	        return;

void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==1462)
    {
        if(frame==32)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1463)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }

}

void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==1467)
    {

    	void self = getlocalvar("self");

	if (frame == 1){	
	changeentityproperty(self, "antigravity", 0.97);
	}
	else if (frame == 24){	
	changeentityproperty(self, "antigravity", 0);
	changeentityproperty(self, "subject_to_screen", 1);
	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1468)
    {

    	void self = getlocalvar("self");

	if (frame == 0){	
	changeentityproperty(self, "antigravity", 0.2);

	}
	else if (frame == 1){	
	changeentityproperty(self, "antigravity", 0);

	}
	        return;

	changeentityproperty(self, "antigravity", 0);
	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1473)
    {


    	void self = getlocalvar("self");
 	void Player = getlocalvar("attacker");
	int  PIndex = getentityproperty(Player,"playerindex");
    	int Score = getplayerproperty(PIndex, "score");

	if (frame == 0){
	changeplayerproperty(PIndex, "score", Score+1);
changeentityproperty(self, "candamage", openborconstant("TYPE_ENEMY")-openborconstant("TYPE_PLAYER"));
	changeentityproperty(self, "antigravity", 0);
	}

	else if (frame == 1){	
	changeentityproperty(self, "type", 0);


	}
	        if(frame==14)
        {
            spawnbind("explosion_safe", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==15)
        {
            killentity(getlocalvar("self"));
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1474)

      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index
    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

     if (frame ==0){
	changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
     if (frame ==20){
      	setdrawmethod(self, 1, 512, 512, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1);
	setentityvar(self, 1, openborvariant("elapsed_time"));
	
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            spawnbind("mutagen_effect", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1514)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");


     if (frame ==0){
	changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
	setdrawmethod(self, 0);
    	}

	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1517)
    {

 if(frame == 1){
   void self = getlocalvar("self");
   int PIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex");
   int HPs = getglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs");

   if(HPs!=NULL()){
     changeentityproperty(self, "health", HPs);
     setglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs", NULL());
   }
 }
        return;
    }

}

    }

    	if (frame ==0){
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1692)
    {
        if(frame==6)
        {
            spawn01("scale_ball_good", 8, 33, 1);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1693)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");
      	int iPIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex"); //Get player index
    	int Player = getplayerproperty(iPIndex, "entity");

     if (frame ==0){
	changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
      	changeentityproperty(Player, "noaicontrol", 0);
    	}
     if (frame ==20){
      	setdrawmethod(self, 1, 512, 512, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1);
	setentityvar(self, 1, openborvariant("elapsed_time"));
	
    	}
	        if(frame==0)
        {
            spawnbind("mutagen_effect", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1694)
    {

      	void self = getlocalvar("self");


     if (frame ==0){
	changeentityproperty(self, "velocity", 0, 0, 0);
	setdrawmethod(self, 0);
    	}

	        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==1697)
    {

 if(frame == 1){
   void self = getlocalvar("self");
   int PIndex = getentityproperty(self,"playerindex");
   int HPs = getglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs");

   if(HPs!=NULL()){
     changeentityproperty(self, "health", HPs);
     setglobalvar(PIndex+"HPs", NULL());
   }
 }
        return;

    }
